	boolchan:=make(chan bool,1)
	go func() {
		for  {
			select {
			case <-rf.stopSignal:{
				boolchan<-false
				return
			}
			case <-toleranceTimer.C:{
				boolchan<-false
				return
			}
			default:
				{
					//call100ms
					ok := rf.peers[server].Call("Raft.RequestVote", args, reply)
					boolchan<-ok
				}
			}
		}
	}()

	for   {
		select {
			case ok:=<-boolchan:{
				if !ok{
					time.Sleep(10*time.Millisecond)
					DPrintf("[rf %d][retry send request vote][target %d]",rf.me,server)
					continue
				}else {
					return true
				}
			}
			case <-rf.stopSignal:
				return false
			case <-toleranceTimer.C:
				return false

		}
	}
